\DoxyCodeLine{4203 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4204 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> Optimization flag. Registers used by TWIS are shared by other peripherals. Normally, during initialization driver tries to clear all registers to known state before doing the initialization itself. This gives initialization safe procedure, no matter when it would be called. If you activate TWIS only once and do never uninitialize it -\/ set this flag to 1 what gives more optimal code.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4205 }

\DoxyCodeLine{5770 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> Optimization flag. Registers used by TWIS are shared by other peripherals. Normally, during initialization driver tries to clear all registers to known state before doing the initialization itself. This gives initialization safe procedure, no matter when it would be called. If you activate TWIS only once and do never uninitialize it -\/ set this flag to 1 what gives more optimal code.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5771 }

\DoxyCodeLine{6389 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> Processing all events from the interrupt level adds requirement not to call any functions that modifies the USBD library state from the context higher than USB interrupt context.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{6663 \textcolor{comment}{// <h> Pages -\/ Virtual page settings}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6664 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6665 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> Configure the number of virtual pages to use and their size.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6666 \textcolor{comment}{//==========================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6667 \textcolor{comment}{// <o> FDS\_VIRTUAL\_PAGES -\/ Number of virtual flash pages to use. }}
\DoxyCodeLine{6668 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> One of the virtual pages is reserved by the system for garbage collection.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6669 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> Therefore, the minimum is two virtual pages: one page to store data and one page to be used by the system for garbage collection.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6670 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> The total amount of flash memory that is used by FDS amounts to @ref FDS\_VIRTUAL\_PAGES * @ref FDS\_VIRTUAL\_PAGE\_SIZE * 4 bytes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6671 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6672 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef FDS\_VIRTUAL\_PAGES}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6673 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FDS\_VIRTUAL\_PAGES 3}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6674 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6675 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6676 \textcolor{comment}{// <o> FDS\_VIRTUAL\_PAGE\_SIZE  -\/ The size of a virtual flash page.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6677  }
\DoxyCodeLine{6678 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6679 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> Expressed in number of 4-\/byte words.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6680 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> By default, a virtual page is the same size as a physical page.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6681 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> The size of a virtual page must be a multiple of the size of a physical page.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6682 \textcolor{comment}{// <1024=> 1024 }}
\DoxyCodeLine{6683 \textcolor{comment}{// <2048=> 2048 }}
\DoxyCodeLine{6684 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6685 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef FDS\_VIRTUAL\_PAGE\_SIZE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6686 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FDS\_VIRTUAL\_PAGE\_SIZE 1024}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6687 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6688 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6689 \textcolor{comment}{// <o> FDS\_VIRTUAL\_PAGES\_RESERVED -\/ The number of virtual flash pages that are used by other modules. }}
\DoxyCodeLine{6690 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> FDS module stores its data in the last pages of the flash memory.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6691 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> By setting this value, you can move flash end address used by the FDS.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{7169 \textcolor{comment}{// <o> MEASUREMENT\_PERIOD -\/ Single measurement period. }}
\DoxyCodeLine{7170 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> Time of a single measurement can be calculated as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7171 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> T = (1/2)*MEASUREMENT\_PERIOD*(1/f\_OSC) where f\_OSC = I\_SOURCE / (2C*(VUP-\/VDOWN) ).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7172 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> I\_SOURCE, VUP, and VDOWN are values used to initialize COMP and C is the capacitance of the used pad.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7173 }
\DoxyCodeLine{7174 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef MEASUREMENT\_PERIOD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7175 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define MEASUREMENT\_PERIOD 20}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7176 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7177 }
\DoxyCodeLine{7178 \textcolor{comment}{// </e>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7179 }
\DoxyCodeLine{7180 \textcolor{comment}{// </e>}}

\DoxyCodeLine{7217 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> Increase this value if events frequently return the @ref NRF\_ERROR\_TIMEOUT error.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7218 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> The SoftDevice might fail to schedule flash access due to high BLE activity.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7219 }

\DoxyCodeLine{7223 }

\DoxyCodeLine{7225 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> This value must be a multiple of four.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7226 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> Lowering this value can increase the chances of the SoftDevice being able to execute flash operations in between radio activity.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7227 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> This value is bound by the maximum number of bytes that can be written to flash in a single call to @ref sd\_flash\_write.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7228 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> That is 1024 bytes for nRF51 ICs and 4096 bytes for nRF52 ICs.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{7654 \textcolor{comment}{//==========================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7655 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef NRF\_LOG\_BACKEND\_RTT\_ENABLED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7656 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define NRF\_LOG\_BACKEND\_RTT\_ENABLED 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7657 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7658 \textcolor{comment}{// <o> NRF\_LOG\_BACKEND\_RTT\_TEMP\_BUFFER\_SIZE -\/ Size of buffer for partially processed strings. }}
\DoxyCodeLine{7659 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> Size of the buffer is a trade-\/off between RAM usage and processing.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7660 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> if buffer is smaller then strings will often be fragmented.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7661 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> It is recommended to use size which will fit typical log and only the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7662 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> longer one will be fragmented.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7663 }
\DoxyCodeLine{7664 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef NRF\_LOG\_BACKEND\_RTT\_TEMP\_BUFFER\_SIZE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7665 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define NRF\_LOG\_BACKEND\_RTT\_TEMP\_BUFFER\_SIZE 64}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7666 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7667 }
\DoxyCodeLine{7668 \textcolor{comment}{// <o> NRF\_LOG\_BACKEND\_RTT\_TX\_RETRY\_DELAY\_MS -\/ Period before retrying writing to RTT }}
\DoxyCodeLine{7669 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef NRF\_LOG\_BACKEND\_RTT\_TX\_RETRY\_DELAY\_MS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7670 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define NRF\_LOG\_BACKEND\_RTT\_TX\_RETRY\_DELAY\_MS 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7671 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7672 }
\DoxyCodeLine{7673 \textcolor{comment}{// <o> NRF\_LOG\_BACKEND\_RTT\_TX\_RETRY\_CNT -\/ Writing to RTT retries. }}
\DoxyCodeLine{7674 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> If RTT fails to accept any new data after retries}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7675 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> module assumes that host is not active and on next}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7676 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> request it will perform only one write attempt.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7677 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> On successful writing, module assumes that host is active}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7678 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> and scheme with retry is applied again.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7679 }
\DoxyCodeLine{7680 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef NRF\_LOG\_BACKEND\_RTT\_TX\_RETRY\_CNT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7681 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define NRF\_LOG\_BACKEND\_RTT\_TX\_RETRY\_CNT 3}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7682 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7683 }
\DoxyCodeLine{7684 \textcolor{comment}{// </e>}}

\DoxyCodeLine{7735 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7736 \textcolor{comment}{// <h> Log message pool -\/ Configuration of log message pool}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7737 }
\DoxyCodeLine{7738 \textcolor{comment}{//==========================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7739 \textcolor{comment}{// <o> NRF\_LOG\_MSGPOOL\_ELEMENT\_SIZE -\/ Size of a single element in the pool of memory objects. }}
\DoxyCodeLine{7740 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> If a small value is set, then performance of logs processing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7741 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> is degraded because data is fragmented. Bigger value impacts}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7742 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> RAM memory utilization. The size is set to fit a message with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7743 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> a timestamp and up to 2 arguments in a single memory object.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7744 }
\DoxyCodeLine{7745 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef NRF\_LOG\_MSGPOOL\_ELEMENT\_SIZE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7746 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define NRF\_LOG\_MSGPOOL\_ELEMENT\_SIZE 20}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7747 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7748 }
\DoxyCodeLine{7749 \textcolor{comment}{// <o> NRF\_LOG\_MSGPOOL\_ELEMENT\_COUNT -\/ Number of elements in the pool of memory objects }}
\DoxyCodeLine{7750 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> If a small value is set, then it may lead to a deadlock}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7751 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> in certain cases if backend has high latency and holds}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7752 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> multiple messages for long time. Bigger value impacts}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7753 \textcolor{comment}{// <i> RAM memory usage.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7754 }
\DoxyCodeLine{7755 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef NRF\_LOG\_MSGPOOL\_ELEMENT\_COUNT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7756 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define NRF\_LOG\_MSGPOOL\_ELEMENT\_COUNT 8}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7757 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7758 }
